# IPUMS DHS Variables — Household Members
Unit of analysis: `household_members`  
Total variables: 2494  
Topic groups: 82  

**[preselected]** = IPUMS includes this variable in every extract automatically.  
**Availability** column shows latest survey year per country (2-letter IPUMS code). Full data in references/dhs_availability.json.
